### 2.2 λ¬Έν•­ κµ¬μ΅° λ° κ°€μ¤‘μΉ μ‹μ¤ν…

#### κ°•μ μ„ νƒν• λ¬Έν•­ (A/B μ„ νƒ)


### 2.3 μ μ λ„μ  μ•κ³ λ¦¬μ¦

```typescript
// μ μ μ μ© ν•¨μ
function applyWeights(currentScores, selectedWeights) {
    const updatedScores = { ...currentScores };
    
    for (const [dimension, value] of selectedWeights) {
        // μ„ νƒλ μµμ…μ κ°€μ¤‘μΉλ¥Ό ν•΄λ‹Ή μ°¨μ›μ— λ„μ 
        updatedScores[dimension] = (updatedScores[dimension] || 0) + value;
    }
    
    return updatedScores;
}
```

```
β”‚      + (0.71Γ—0.60) + (1.00Γ—0.90) + (0.63Γ—0.70)                    β”‚
β”‚      = 2.70                                                        β”‚
β”‚                                                                    β”‚
β”‚  ||A|| = β(0.40Β² + 0.91Β² + ... + 0.63Β²) = 1.89                    β”‚
β”‚  ||B|| = β(0.30Β² + 0.85Β² + ... + 0.70Β²) = 1.68                    β”‚
β”‚                                                                    β”‚
β”‚  similarity = 2.70 / (1.89 Γ— 1.68) = 0.85 (85% λ§¤μΉ­)              β”‚
β”‚                                                                    β”‚
β””β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”€β”
```

## λ¶€λ΅: κΈ°μ  μƒμ„Έ

### A. ν•µμ‹¬ μ•κ³ λ¦¬μ¦ μ½”λ“ μ¤λ‹ν«

#### μ½”μ‚¬μΈ μ μ‚¬λ„ κ³„μ‚°

```typescript
function cosineSimilarity(
  vecA: Record<Dim, number>, 
  vecB: Partial<Record<Dim, number>>
): number {
  const DIMS = ['R', 'I', 'A', 'S', 'E', 'C'];
  let dot = 0, a2 = 0, b2 = 0;
  
  DIMS.forEach((dim) => {
    const a = vecA[dim] || 0;
    const b = vecB[dim] || 0;
    dot += a * b;
    a2 += a * a;
    b2 += b * b;
  });
  
  const denom = Math.sqrt(a2) * Math.sqrt(b2);
  return denom === 0 ? 0 : dot / denom;
}
```

#### μ μ μ •κ·ν™”

```typescript
function normalizeScores(scores: Record<Dim, number>): Record<Dim, number> {
  const DIMS = ['R', 'I', 'A', 'S', 'E', 'C'];
  const values = DIMS.map((d) => scores[d] || 0);
  const maxVal = Math.max(1, ...values);
  
  const normalized: Record<Dim, number> = {} as Record<Dim, number>;
  DIMS.forEach((d) => {
    normalized[d] = (scores[d] || 0) / maxVal;
  });
  
  return normalized;
}
```
